 			// decrypt helper function
 		function decryptCharcode(n,start,end,offset) {
 			n = n + offset;
 			if (offset > 0 && n > end) {
 				n = start + (n - end - 1);
 			} else if (offset < 0 && n < start) {
 				n = end - (start - n - 1);
 			}
 			return String.fromCharCode(n);
 		}
 			// decrypt string
 		function decryptString(enc,offset) {
 			var dec = "";
 			var len = enc.length;
 			for(var i=0; i < len; i++) {
 				var n = enc.charCodeAt(i);
 				if (n >= 0x2B && n <= 0x3A) {
 					dec += decryptCharcode(n,0x2B,0x3A,offset);	// 0-9 . , - + / :
 				} else if (n >= 0x40 && n <= 0x5A) {
 					dec += decryptCharcode(n,0x40,0x5A,offset);	// A-Z @
 				} else if (n >= 0x61 && n <= 0x7A) {
 					dec += decryptCharcode(n,0x61,0x7A,offset);	// a-z
 				} else {
 					dec += enc.charAt(i);
 				}
 			}
 			return dec;
 		}
 			// decrypt spam-protected emails
 		function linkTo_UnCryptMailto(s) {
 			location.href = decryptString(s,-1);
 		}

 document.createElement( 'picture' );/*! EnhanceJS: a progressive enhancement boilerplate. Copyright 2014 @scottjehl, Filament Group, Inc. Licensed MIT */
 (function (window, undefined) {
 
 	// Enable JS strict mode
 	"use strict";
 	var setTimeout = window.setTimeout;
 
 	var enhance = {};
 
 	// Define some variables to be used throughout this file
 	var doc = window.document,
 		docElem = doc.documentElement,
 		head = doc.head || doc.getElementsByTagName("head")[0],
 	// this references a meta tag's name whose content attribute should define the path to the full CSS file for the site
 		fullCSSKey = "fullcss",
 	// this references a meta tag's name whose content attribute should define the path to the enhanced JS file for the site (delivered to qualified browsers)
 		fullJSKey = "fulljs",
 	// classes to be added to the HTML element in qualified browsers
 		htmlClasses = ["enhanced"];
 
 	/* Some commonly used functions - delete anything you don't need! */
 
 	// loadJS: load a JS file asynchronously. Included from https://github.com/filamentgroup/loadJS/
 	function loadJS(src) {
 		var ref = window.document.getElementsByTagName("script")[0];
 		var script = window.document.createElement("script");
 		script.src = src;
 		script.async = true;
 		ref.parentNode.insertBefore(script, ref);
 		return script;
 	}
 
 	// expose it
 	enhance.loadJS = loadJS;
 
 	// loadCSS: load a CSS file asynchronously. Included from https://github.com/filamentgroup/loadCSS/
 	function loadCSS(href, before, media) {
 		// Arguments explained:
 		// `href` is the URL for your CSS file.
 		// `before` optionally defines the element we'll use as a reference for injecting our <link>
 		// By default, `before` uses the first <script> element in the page.
 		// However, since the order in which stylesheets are referenced matters, you might need a more specific location in your document.
 		// If so, pass a different reference element to the `before` argument and it'll insert before that instead
 		// note: `insertBefore` is used instead of `appendChild`, for safety re: http://www.paulirish.com/2011/surefire-dom-element-insertion/
 		var ss = window.document.createElement("link");
 		var ref = before || window.document.getElementsByTagName("script")[0];
 		var sheets = window.document.styleSheets;
 		ss.rel = "stylesheet";
 		ss.href = href;
 		// temporarily, set media to something non-matching to ensure it'll fetch without blocking render
 		ss.media = "only x";
 		// inject link
 		ref.parentNode.insertBefore(ss, ref);
 		// This function sets the link's media back to `all` so that the stylesheet applies once it loads
 		// It is designed to poll until document.styleSheets includes the new sheet.
 		function toggleMedia() {
 			var defined;
 			for (var i = 0; i < sheets.length; i++) {
 				if (sheets[i].href && sheets[i].href.indexOf(href) > -1) {
 					defined = true;
 				}
 			}
 			if (defined) {
 				ss.media = media || "all";
 			}
 			else {
 				setTimeout(toggleMedia);
 			}
 		}
 
 		toggleMedia();
 		return ss;
 	}
 
 	// expose it
 	enhance.loadCSS = loadCSS;
 
 	// getMeta function: get a meta tag by name
 	// NOTE: meta tag must be in the HTML source before this script is included in order to guarantee it'll be found
 	function getMeta(metaname) {
 		var metas = window.document.getElementsByTagName("meta");
 		var meta;
 		for (var i = 0; i < metas.length; i++) {
 			if (metas[i].name && metas[i].name === metaname) {
 				meta = metas[i];
 				break;
 			}
 		}
 		return meta;
 	}
 
 	// expose it
 	enhance.getMeta = getMeta;
 
 	// cookie function from https://github.com/filamentgroup/cookie/
 	function cookie(name, value, days) {
 		var expires;
 		// if value is undefined, get the cookie value
 		if (value === undefined) {
 			var cookiestring = "; " + window.document.cookie;
 			var cookies = cookiestring.split("; " + name + "=");
 			if (cookies.length == 2) {
 				return cookies.pop().split(";").shift();
 			}
 			return null;
 		}
 		else {
 			// if value is a false boolean, we'll treat that as a delete
 			if (value === false) {
 				days = -1;
 			}
 			if (days) {
 				var date = new Date();
 				date.setTime(date.getTime() + ( days * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000 ));
 				expires = "; expires=" + date.toGMTString();
 			}
 			else {
 				expires = "";
 			}
 			window.document.cookie = name + "=" + value + expires + "; path=/";
 		}
 	}
 
 	// expose it
 	enhance.cookie = cookie;
 
 	/* Enhancements for all browsers - qualified or not */
 
 	/* Load non-critical CSS async on first visit:
 	 On first visit to the site, the critical CSS for each template should be inlined in the head, while the full CSS for the site should be requested async and cached for later use.
 	 A meta tag with a name matching the fullCSSKey should have a content attribute referencing the path to the full CSS file for the site.
 	 If no cookie is set to specify that the full CSS has already been fetched, load it asynchronously and set the cookie.
 	 Once the cookie is set, the full CSS is assumed to be in cache, and the server-side templates should reference the full CSS directly from the head of the page with a link element, in place of inline critical styles.
 	 */
 	var fullCSS = getMeta(fullCSSKey);
 	if (fullCSS && !cookie(fullCSSKey)) {
 		loadCSS(fullCSS.content);
 		// set cookie to mark this file fetched
 		cookie(fullCSSKey, "true", 7);
 	}
 
 	/* Enhancements for qualified browsers - "Cutting the Mustard"
 	 Add your qualifications for major browser experience divisions here.
 	 For example, you might choose to only enhance browsers that support document.querySelector (IE8+, etc).
 	 Use case will vary.
 	 */
 	if (!( "querySelector" in doc && 'localStorage' in window && 'addEventListener' in window)) {
 		//if( !( "querySelector" in doc) ){
 		// basic browsers: last stop here!
 		return;
 	}
 
 	// From here on we're dealing with qualified browsers.
 
 	// Add scoping classes to HTML element: useful for upgrading the presentation of elements that will be enhanced with JS behavior
 	docElem.className += " " + htmlClasses.join(" ");
 
 	/* Load JavaScript enhancements in one request.
 	 Your DOM framework and dependent component scripts should be concatenated and minified into one file that we'll load dynamically (keep that file as small as possible!)
 	 A meta tag with a name matching the fullJSKey should have a content attribute referencing the path to this JavaScript file.
 	 */
 	var fullJS = getMeta(fullJSKey);
 	if (fullJS) {
 		loadJS(fullJS.content);
 	}
 
 	// expose the 'enhance' object globally. Use it to expose anything in here that's useful to other parts of your application.
 	window.enhance = enhance;
 
 }(this));

      <article class="m-intro-home__item">
       <div class="m-intro-home__background" style="background-image: url('/fileadmin/user_upload_bund/bilder/startseite/wasser_kampagne_slider.jpg')">
       </div>
       <div class="m-intro-home__content">
        <h2 class="m-intro-home__headline ">
         Rette unser Wasser!
        </h2>
        <p class="rte-paragraph rte-paragraph__intro">
         Unser Wasser ist in akuter Gefahr: Die mächtige Lobby von Agrarchemie und Industrie will den EU-Wasserschutz schwächen. Das darf nicht passieren. Schicken Sie jetzt eine Nachricht an Bundesumweltministerin Schulze!
        </p>
        <p class="rte-paragraph rte-paragraph__intro">
         <a class="rte-anchor rte-anchor--button rte-anchor--button__btnRed" href="https://aktion.bund.net/rette-unser-wasser?utm_source=website&amp;utm_content=slider&amp;utm_campaign=WRRL&amp;utm_medium=website" target="_blank">
          Jetzt mitmachen!
         </a>
        </p>
       </div>
      </article>
      <article class="m-intro-home__item">
       <div class="m-intro-home__background" style="background-image: url('/fileadmin/user_upload_bund/bilder/startseite/kohle-stoppen.jpg')">
       </div>
       <div class="m-intro-home__content">
        <h2 class="m-intro-home__headline ">
         Demo: Stop Kohle!
        </h2>
        <p class="rte-paragraph rte-paragraph__intro">
         Das Endspiel um die Kohle beginnt. Am 24. Juni senden wir mit unseren Händen ein klares Signal: Stop Kohle! Gemeinsam zeigen wir: Die übergroße Mehrheit der Bevölkerung will beim Klimaschutz endlich Taten sehen.
        </p>
        <p class="rte-paragraph rte-paragraph__intro">
         <a class="rte-anchor rte-anchor--button rte-anchor--button__btnWhite" href="/service/termine/detail/event/demo-stop-kohle/">
          Mehr...
         </a>
        </p>
       </div>

     <section class="m-layout-section m-layout-section__bottomPadding m-layout-section__backgroundLightGrey" id="section4396">
      <div class="g-container">
       <div class="m-content-donationslider ">
        <div class="m-content-donationslider--sliderWrapper">
         <div class="m-content-donationslider--sliderItem">
          <img class="m-content-donationslider--image" src="/fileadmin/user_upload_bund/bilder/startseite/sommertipps_teaser.jpg"/>
          <h2 class="rte-heading rte-heading--h3">
           Unsere Sommertipps
          </h2>
          <p class="rte-paragraph">
           So wird der Sommer noch schöner: Mit unseren Sommertipps lernen Sie u.a., wie Sie umweltfreundlich grillen, Sonnenbrand auf natürliche Weise vorbeugen oder ungetrübt in Seen und Flüssen baden können.
          </p>
          <a class="rte-anchor rte-anchor--button rte-anchor--button__btnGreen rte-anchor--button__btnBlock" href="https://www.bund.net/bund-tipps/oekotipps/tip-topic/sommer/" target="_self">
           Weiterlesen
          </a>
         </div>
         <div class="m-content-donationslider--sliderItem">
          <img class="m-content-donationslider--image" src="/fileadmin/user_upload_bund/bilder/startseite/bienen_start.jpg"/>
          <h2 class="rte-heading rte-heading--h3">
           A Place to Bee
          </h2>
          <p class="rte-paragraph">
           Mit 3.500 Häkelbienen im Gepäck haben wir mehr als 180.000 Unterschriften zum Schutz von Bienen und anderen Bestäubern an das Bundesumweltministerium übergeben. Nun ist die Politik am Zug.
          </p>
          <a class="rte-anchor rte-anchor--button rte-anchor--button__btnGreen rte-anchor--button__btnBlock" href="https://aktion.bund.net/a-place-to-bee" target="_blank">
           Weiterlesen
          </a>
         </div>
         <div class="m-content-donationslider--sliderItem">
          <img class="m-content-donationslider--image" src="/fileadmin/user_upload_bund/bilder/startseite/pestizidfreie_kommune_klein.jpg"/>
          <h2 class="rte-heading rte-heading--h3">
           Pestizidfreie Städte
          </h2>
          <p class="rte-paragraph">
           Bisher haben sich 210 Städte und Gemeinden entschieden, ihre Grünflächen ohne Pestizide oder mindestens ohne Glyphosat zu bewirtschaften. Wir haben eine interaktive Karte dieser Orte erstellt.
          </p>
          <a class="rte-anchor rte-anchor--button rte-anchor--button__btnGreen rte-anchor--button__btnBlock" href="/umweltgifte/pestizide/pestizidfreie-kommune/">
           weiterlesen
          </a>
         </div>
         <div class="m-content-donationslider--sliderItem">
          <img class="m-content-donationslider--image" src="/fileadmin/_processed_/2/7/csm_denkmal_aktiv_schueler_unterricht_4be4e52150.jpg"/>
          <h2 class="rte-heading rte-heading--h3">
           BUND-Umweltbildung
          </h2>
          <p class="rte-paragraph">
           Bildung ist ein zentraler Aspekt erfolgreicher Umweltarbeit. Im Fokus des BUND steht die Bildung für nachhaltige Entwicklung – für jede Altersstufe. Erfahren Sie mehr über unsere Projekte in der Umweltbildung!
          </p>
          <a class="rte-anchor rte-anchor--button rte-anchor--button__btnGreen rte-anchor--button__btnBlock" href="/bund-tipps/natur-erfahren/umweltbildung/">
           Weiterlesen
          </a>
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </section>
     <section class="m-layout-section m-layout-section__bottomPadding m-layout-section__backgroundLightGrey" id="section5313">
      <div class="g-container g-container__offGrid ">
       <h2 class="rte-heading rte-heading--h2 rte-heading__centered">
        Aktuelles
       </h2>
       <div class="m-layout-2col m-layout-2col__noBorder m-layout-2col__smallPadding">
        <div class="m-layout-2col--content m-layout-2col--content__mainContent">
         <div class="m-layout-grid m-layout-grid__dashboardGrid">
          <article class="m-content-dashboardbox m-content-dashboardbox__publicationBox">
           <a class="m-content-dashboardbox--anchor tx-bundpool-topic-set" href="/service/publikationen/detail/publication/alles-im-fluss/">
            <div class="m-content-dashboardbox--imageWrapper">
             <div class="m-content-dashboardbox--image" style="background-image:url('/fileadmin/user_upload_bund/bilder/publikationen/flussbroschuere.jpg');">
             </div>
            </div>
            <div class="m-content-dashboardbox--contentWrapper">
             <p class="rte-paragraph rte-paragraph__caption">
              22. Juni 2018

            </a>
           </span>
           <span class="rte-paragraph rte-paragraph__caption rte-image--imageCaption">

    /*<![CDATA[*/
 /*_scriptCode*/
 
 			// decrypt helper function
 		function decryptCharcode(n,start,end,offset) {
 			n = n + offset;
 			if (offset > 0 && n > end) {
 				n = start + (n - end - 1);
 			} else if (offset < 0 && n < start) {
 				n = end - (start - n - 1);
 			}
 			return String.fromCharCode(n);
 		}
 			// decrypt string
 		function decryptString(enc,offset) {
 			var dec = "";
 			var len = enc.length;
 			for(var i=0; i < len; i++) {
 				var n = enc.charCodeAt(i);
 				if (n >= 0x2B && n <= 0x3A) {
 					dec += decryptCharcode(n,0x2B,0x3A,offset);	// 0-9 . , - + / :
 				} else if (n >= 0x40 && n <= 0x5A) {
 					dec += decryptCharcode(n,0x40,0x5A,offset);	// A-Z @
 				} else if (n >= 0x61 && n <= 0x7A) {
 					dec += decryptCharcode(n,0x61,0x7A,offset);	// a-z
 				} else {
 					dec += enc.charAt(i);
 				}
 			}
 			return dec;
 		}
 			// decrypt spam-protected emails
 		function linkTo_UnCryptMailto(s) {
 			location.href = decryptString(s,-1);
 		}
 		
 
 /*TS_inlineJS*/
 
 document.createElement( 'picture' );/*! EnhanceJS: a progressive enhancement boilerplate. Copyright 2014 @scottjehl, Filament Group, Inc. Licensed MIT */
 (function (window, undefined) {
 
 	// Enable JS strict mode
 	"use strict";
 	var setTimeout = window.setTimeout;
 
 	var enhance = {};
 
 	// Define some variables to be used throughout this file
 	var doc = window.document,
 		docElem = doc.documentElement,
 		head = doc.head || doc.getElementsByTagName("head")[0],
 	// this references a meta tag's name whose content attribute should define the path to the full CSS file for the site
 		fullCSSKey = "fullcss",
 	// this references a meta tag's name whose content attribute should define the path to the enhanced JS file for the site (delivered to qualified browsers)
 		fullJSKey = "fulljs",
 	// classes to be added to the HTML element in qualified browsers
 		htmlClasses = ["enhanced"];
 
 	/* Some commonly used functions - delete anything you don't need! */
 
 	// loadJS: load a JS file asynchronously. Included from https://github.com/filamentgroup/loadJS/
 	function loadJS(src) {
 		var ref = window.document.getElementsByTagName("script")[0];
 		var script = window.document.createElement("script");
 		script.src = src;
 		script.async = true;
 		ref.parentNode.insertBefore(script, ref);
 		return script;
 	}
 
 	// expose it
 	enhance.loadJS = loadJS;
 
 	// loadCSS: load a CSS file asynchronously. Included from https://github.com/filamentgroup/loadCSS/
 	function loadCSS(href, before, media) {
 		// Arguments explained:
 		// `href` is the URL for your CSS file.
 		// `before` optionally defines the element we'll use as a reference for injecting our <link>
 		// By default, `before` uses the first <script> element in the page.
 		// However, since the order in which stylesheets are referenced matters, you might need a more specific location in your document.
 		// If so, pass a different reference element to the `before` argument and it'll insert before that instead
 		// note: `insertBefore` is used instead of `appendChild`, for safety re: http://www.paulirish.com/2011/surefire-dom-element-insertion/
 		var ss = window.document.createElement("link");
 		var ref = before || window.document.getElementsByTagName("script")[0];
 		var sheets = window.document.styleSheets;
 		ss.rel = "stylesheet";
 		ss.href = href;
 		// temporarily, set media to something non-matching to ensure it'll fetch without blocking render
 		ss.media = "only x";
 		// inject link
 		ref.parentNode.insertBefore(ss, ref);
 		// This function sets the link's media back to `all` so that the stylesheet applies once it loads
 		// It is designed to poll until document.styleSheets includes the new sheet.
 		function toggleMedia() {
 			var defined;
 			for (var i = 0; i < sheets.length; i++) {
 				if (sheets[i].href && sheets[i].href.indexOf(href) > -1) {
 					defined = true;
 				}
 			}
 			if (defined) {
 				ss.media = media || "all";
 			}
 			else {
 				setTimeout(toggleMedia);
 			}
 		}
 
 		toggleMedia();
 		return ss;
 	}
 
 	// expose it
 	enhance.loadCSS = loadCSS;
 
 	// getMeta function: get a meta tag by name
 	// NOTE: meta tag must be in the HTML source before this script is included in order to guarantee it'll be found
 	function getMeta(metaname) {
 		var metas = window.document.getElementsByTagName("meta");
 		var meta;
 		for (var i = 0; i < metas.length; i++) {
 			if (metas[i].name && metas[i].name === metaname) {
 				meta = metas[i];
 				break;
 			}
 		}
 		return meta;
 	}
 
 	// expose it
 	enhance.getMeta = getMeta;
 
 	// cookie function from https://github.com/filamentgroup/cookie/
 	function cookie(name, value, days) {
 		var expires;
 		// if value is undefined, get the cookie value
 		if (value === undefined) {
 			var cookiestring = "; " + window.document.cookie;
 			var cookies = cookiestring.split("; " + name + "=");
 			if (cookies.length == 2) {
 				return cookies.pop().split(";").shift();
 			}
 			return null;
 		}
 		else {
 			// if value is a false boolean, we'll treat that as a delete
 			if (value === false) {
 				days = -1;
 			}
 			if (days) {
 				var date = new Date();
 				date.setTime(date.getTime() + ( days * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000 ));
 				expires = "; expires=" + date.toGMTString();
 			}
 			else {
 				expires = "";
 			}
 			window.document.cookie = name + "=" + value + expires + "; path=/";
 		}
 	}
 
 	// expose it
 	enhance.cookie = cookie;
 
 	/* Enhancements for all browsers - qualified or not */
 
 	/* Load non-critical CSS async on first visit:
 	 On first visit to the site, the critical CSS for each template should be inlined in the head, while the full CSS for the site should be requested async and cached for later use.
 	 A meta tag with a name matching the fullCSSKey should have a content attribute referencing the path to the full CSS file for the site.
 	 If no cookie is set to specify that the full CSS has already been fetched, load it asynchronously and set the cookie.
 	 Once the cookie is set, the full CSS is assumed to be in cache, and the server-side templates should reference the full CSS directly from the head of the page with a link element, in place of inline critical styles.
 	 */
 	var fullCSS = getMeta(fullCSSKey);
 	if (fullCSS && !cookie(fullCSSKey)) {
 		loadCSS(fullCSS.content);
 		// set cookie to mark this file fetched
 		cookie(fullCSSKey, "true", 7);
 	}
 
 	/* Enhancements for qualified browsers - "Cutting the Mustard"
 	 Add your qualifications for major browser experience divisions here.
 	 For example, you might choose to only enhance browsers that support document.querySelector (IE8+, etc).
 	 Use case will vary.
 	 */
 	if (!( "querySelector" in doc && 'localStorage' in window && 'addEventListener' in window)) {
 		//if( !( "querySelector" in doc) ){
 		// basic browsers: last stop here!
 		return;
 	}
 
 	// From here on we're dealing with qualified browsers.
 
 	// Add scoping classes to HTML element: useful for upgrading the presentation of elements that will be enhanced with JS behavior
 	docElem.className += " " + htmlClasses.join(" ");
 
 	/* Load JavaScript enhancements in one request.
 	 Your DOM framework and dependent component scripts should be concatenated and minified into one file that we'll load dynamically (keep that file as small as possible!)
 	 A meta tag with a name matching the fullJSKey should have a content attribute referencing the path to this JavaScript file.
 	 */
 	var fullJS = getMeta(fullJSKey);
 	if (fullJS) {
 		loadJS(fullJS.content);
 	}
 
 	// expose the 'enhance' object globally. Use it to expose anything in here that's useful to other parts of your application.
 	window.enhance = enhance;

         Rette unser Wasser!
        </h2>

        </p>

         </a>

     <section class="m-layout-section m-layout-section__bottomPadding m-layout-section__backgroundLightGrey" id="section4396">
      <div class="g-container">
       <div class="m-content-donationslider ">
        <div class="m-content-donationslider--sliderWrapper">
         <div class="m-content-donationslider--sliderItem">
          <img class="m-content-donationslider--image" src="/fileadmin/user_upload_bund/bilder/startseite/sommertipps_teaser.jpg"/>
          <h2 class="rte-heading rte-heading--h3">
           Unsere Sommertipps
          </h2>
          <p class="rte-paragraph">
           So wird der Sommer noch schöner: Mit unseren Sommertipps lernen Sie u.a., wie Sie umweltfreundlich grillen, Sonnenbrand auf natürliche Weise vorbeugen oder ungetrübt in Seen und Flüssen baden können.
          </p>
          <a class="rte-anchor rte-anchor--button rte-anchor--button__btnGreen rte-anchor--button__btnBlock" href="https://www.bund.net/bund-tipps/oekotipps/tip-topic/sommer/" target="_self">
           Weiterlesen
          </a>
         </div>
         <div class="m-content-donationslider--sliderItem">
          <img class="m-content-donationslider--image" src="/fileadmin/user_upload_bund/bilder/startseite/bienen_start.jpg"/>
          <h2 class="rte-heading rte-heading--h3">
           A Place to Bee
          </h2>
          <p class="rte-paragraph">
           Mit 3.500 Häkelbienen im Gepäck haben wir mehr als 180.000 Unterschriften zum Schutz von Bienen und anderen Bestäubern an das Bundesumweltministerium übergeben. Nun ist die Politik am Zug.
          </p>
          <a class="rte-anchor rte-anchor--button rte-anchor--button__btnGreen rte-anchor--button__btnBlock" href="https://aktion.bund.net/a-place-to-bee" target="_blank">
           Weiterlesen
          </a>
         </div>
         <div class="m-content-donationslider--sliderItem">
          <img class="m-content-donationslider--image" src="/fileadmin/user_upload_bund/bilder/startseite/pestizidfreie_kommune_klein.jpg"/>
          <h2 class="rte-heading rte-heading--h3">
           Pestizidfreie Städte
          </h2>
          <p class="rte-paragraph">
           Bisher haben sich 210 Städte und Gemeinden entschieden, ihre Grünflächen ohne Pestizide oder mindestens ohne Glyphosat zu bewirtschaften. Wir haben eine interaktive Karte dieser Orte erstellt.
          </p>
          <a class="rte-anchor rte-anchor--button rte-anchor--button__btnGreen rte-anchor--button__btnBlock" href="/umweltgifte/pestizide/pestizidfreie-kommune/">
           weiterlesen
          </a>
         </div>
         <div class="m-content-donationslider--sliderItem">
          <img class="m-content-donationslider--image" src="/fileadmin/_processed_/2/7/csm_denkmal_aktiv_schueler_unterricht_4be4e52150.jpg"/>
          <h2 class="rte-heading rte-heading--h3">
           BUND-Umweltbildung
          </h2>
          <p class="rte-paragraph">
           Bildung ist ein zentraler Aspekt erfolgreicher Umweltarbeit. Im Fokus des BUND steht die Bildung für nachhaltige Entwicklung – für jede Altersstufe. Erfahren Sie mehr über unsere Projekte in der Umweltbildung!
          </p>
          <a class="rte-anchor rte-anchor--button rte-anchor--button__btnGreen rte-anchor--button__btnBlock" href="/bund-tipps/natur-erfahren/umweltbildung/">
           Weiterlesen
          </a>
         </div>

     <section class="themespage-take-action" id="section4498" style="background-image: url('/fileadmin/user_upload_bund/bilder/waelder/keepers_wald_fluss.jpg');">

         <h2 class="rte-heading ">
          BUND-Mitglied werden!
         </h2>
         <div class="ce-textpic ce-left ce-intext">
          <span class="rte-image rte-image__imageLeft ">
           <span class="rte-image--imageWrapper">
            <a href="https://mitglied.bund.net/?wc=21731" target="_blank">

           <span class="rte-paragraph rte-paragraph__caption rte-image--imageCaption">
           </span>
          </span>
          <div class="ce-bodytext">
           <p>
            Wie kann eine tier- und verbraucher­freundliche Agrarwende organisiert werden? Jetzt BUND-Mitglied werden und den Fleischatlas 2018 als Dankeschön erhalten!
           </p>
           <p>
            <a class="rte-anchor rte-anchor--button rte-anchor--button__btnGreen" href="https://mitglied.bund.net/?wc=21731" target="_blank">

           </span>

       <div class="m-layout-grid m-layout-grid__3col m-layout-grid__centeredGrid">
        <div class=" " id="c3914">
         <h2 class="rte-heading ">
          Landesverbände
         </h2>
         <div class="ce-textpic ce-left ce-intext">
          <span class="rte-image rte-image__imageLeft ">
           <span class="rte-image--imageWrapper">
            <a href="/ueber-uns/organisation/landesverbaende/">
             <img alt="" class="rte-image--image" src="/fileadmin/user_upload_bund/bilder/startseite/lv_start_neu.jpg" title=""/>
            </a>
           </span>
           <span class="rte-paragraph rte-paragraph__caption rte-image--imageCaption">
           </span>
          </span>
          <div class="ce-bodytext">
           <p>
            Der BUND ist föderativ orga­nisiert: In jedem Bundesland engagiert sich  ein BUND-Lan­des­­verband für Natur- und Umweltschutz. Erfahren Sie mehr über die regionalen Verbände.
           </p>
           <p>
            <a class="rte-anchor rte-anchor--button rte-anchor--button__btnGreen" href="/ueber-uns/organisation/landesverbaende/">
             Zur Übersicht
            </a>
           </p>
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>
        <div class=" " id="c3911">
         <h2 class="rte-heading ">
          BUND-Stiftung
         </h2>
         <div class="ce-textpic ce-left ce-intext">
          <span class="rte-image rte-image__imageLeft ">
           <span class="rte-image--imageWrapper">
            <a href="/spenden-und-unterstuetzen/weitere-moeglichkeiten/bundstiftung/">

           <span class="rte-paragraph rte-paragraph__caption rte-image--imageCaption">
           </span>
          </span>
          <div class="ce-bodytext">
           <p>
            Mit der BUNDstiftung möchten wir erreichen, dass natürlicher Wildwuchs wieder zum wesentlichen Faktor in  unserer Landschaft wird!
           </p>
           <p>
            <a class="rte-anchor rte-anchor--button rte-anchor--button__btnGreen" href="/spenden-und-unterstuetzen/weitere-moeglichkeiten/bundstiftung/">

 /*_scriptCode*/
 
 			// decrypt helper function
 		function decryptCharcode(n,start,end,offset) {
 			n = n + offset;
 			if (offset > 0 && n > end) {
 				n = start + (n - end - 1);
 			} else if (offset < 0 && n < start) {
 				n = end - (start - n - 1);
 			}
 			return String.fromCharCode(n);
 		}
 			// decrypt string
 		function decryptString(enc,offset) {
 			var dec = "";
 			var len = enc.length;
 			for(var i=0; i < len; i++) {
 				var n = enc.charCodeAt(i);
 				if (n >= 0x2B && n <= 0x3A) {
 					dec += decryptCharcode(n,0x2B,0x3A,offset);	// 0-9 . , - + / :
 				} else if (n >= 0x40 && n <= 0x5A) {
 					dec += decryptCharcode(n,0x40,0x5A,offset);	// A-Z @
 				} else if (n >= 0x61 && n <= 0x7A) {
 					dec += decryptCharcode(n,0x61,0x7A,offset);	// a-z
 				} else {
 					dec += enc.charAt(i);
 				}
 			}
 			return dec;
 		}
 			// decrypt spam-protected emails
 		function linkTo_UnCryptMailto(s) {
 			location.href = decryptString(s,-1);
 		}

 document.createElement( 'picture' );/*! EnhanceJS: a progressive enhancement boilerplate. Copyright 2014 @scottjehl, Filament Group, Inc. Licensed MIT */
 (function (window, undefined) {
 
 	// Enable JS strict mode
 	"use strict";
 	var setTimeout = window.setTimeout;
 
 	var enhance = {};
 
 	// Define some variables to be used throughout this file
 	var doc = window.document,
 		docElem = doc.documentElement,
 		head = doc.head || doc.getElementsByTagName("head")[0],
 	// this references a meta tag's name whose content attribute should define the path to the full CSS file for the site
 		fullCSSKey = "fullcss",
 	// this references a meta tag's name whose content attribute should define the path to the enhanced JS file for the site (delivered to qualified browsers)
 		fullJSKey = "fulljs",
 	// classes to be added to the HTML element in qualified browsers
 		htmlClasses = ["enhanced"];
 
 	/* Some commonly used functions - delete anything you don't need! */
 
 	// loadJS: load a JS file asynchronously. Included from https://github.com/filamentgroup/loadJS/
 	function loadJS(src) {
 		var ref = window.document.getElementsByTagName("script")[0];
 		var script = window.document.createElement("script");
 		script.src = src;
 		script.async = true;
 		ref.parentNode.insertBefore(script, ref);
 		return script;
 	}
 
 	// expose it
 	enhance.loadJS = loadJS;
 
 	// loadCSS: load a CSS file asynchronously. Included from https://github.com/filamentgroup/loadCSS/
 	function loadCSS(href, before, media) {
 		// Arguments explained:
 		// `href` is the URL for your CSS file.
 		// `before` optionally defines the element we'll use as a reference for injecting our <link>
 		// By default, `before` uses the first <script> element in the page.
 		// However, since the order in which stylesheets are referenced matters, you might need a more specific location in your document.
 		// If so, pass a different reference element to the `before` argument and it'll insert before that instead
 		// note: `insertBefore` is used instead of `appendChild`, for safety re: http://www.paulirish.com/2011/surefire-dom-element-insertion/
 		var ss = window.document.createElement("link");
 		var ref = before || window.document.getElementsByTagName("script")[0];
 		var sheets = window.document.styleSheets;
 		ss.rel = "stylesheet";
 		ss.href = href;
 		// temporarily, set media to something non-matching to ensure it'll fetch without blocking render
 		ss.media = "only x";
 		// inject link
 		ref.parentNode.insertBefore(ss, ref);
 		// This function sets the link's media back to `all` so that the stylesheet applies once it loads
 		// It is designed to poll until document.styleSheets includes the new sheet.
 		function toggleMedia() {
 			var defined;
 			for (var i = 0; i < sheets.length; i++) {
 				if (sheets[i].href && sheets[i].href.indexOf(href) > -1) {
 					defined = true;
 				}
 			}
 			if (defined) {
 				ss.media = media || "all";
 			}
 			else {
 				setTimeout(toggleMedia);
 			}
 		}
 
 		toggleMedia();
 		return ss;
 	}
 
 	// expose it
 	enhance.loadCSS = loadCSS;
 
 	// getMeta function: get a meta tag by name
 	// NOTE: meta tag must be in the HTML source before this script is included in order to guarantee it'll be found
 	function getMeta(metaname) {
 		var metas = window.document.getElementsByTagName("meta");
 		var meta;
 		for (var i = 0; i < metas.length; i++) {
 			if (metas[i].name && metas[i].name === metaname) {
 				meta = metas[i];
 				break;
 			}
 		}
 		return meta;
 	}
 
 	// expose it
 	enhance.getMeta = getMeta;
 
 	// cookie function from https://github.com/filamentgroup/cookie/
 	function cookie(name, value, days) {
 		var expires;
 		// if value is undefined, get the cookie value
 		if (value === undefined) {
 			var cookiestring = "; " + window.document.cookie;
 			var cookies = cookiestring.split("; " + name + "=");
 			if (cookies.length == 2) {
 				return cookies.pop().split(";").shift();
 			}
 			return null;
 		}
 		else {
 			// if value is a false boolean, we'll treat that as a delete
 			if (value === false) {
 				days = -1;
 			}
 			if (days) {
 				var date = new Date();
 				date.setTime(date.getTime() + ( days * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000 ));
 				expires = "; expires=" + date.toGMTString();
 			}
 			else {
 				expires = "";
 			}
 			window.document.cookie = name + "=" + value + expires + "; path=/";
 		}
 	}
 
 	// expose it
 	enhance.cookie = cookie;
 
 	/* Enhancements for all browsers - qualified or not */
 
 	/* Load non-critical CSS async on first visit:
 	 On first visit to the site, the critical CSS for each template should be inlined in the head, while the full CSS for the site should be requested async and cached for later use.
 	 A meta tag with a name matching the fullCSSKey should have a content attribute referencing the path to the full CSS file for the site.
 	 If no cookie is set to specify that the full CSS has already been fetched, load it asynchronously and set the cookie.
 	 Once the cookie is set, the full CSS is assumed to be in cache, and the server-side templates should reference the full CSS directly from the head of the page with a link element, in place of inline critical styles.
 	 */
 	var fullCSS = getMeta(fullCSSKey);
 	if (fullCSS && !cookie(fullCSSKey)) {
 		loadCSS(fullCSS.content);
 		// set cookie to mark this file fetched
 		cookie(fullCSSKey, "true", 7);
 	}
 
 	/* Enhancements for qualified browsers - "Cutting the Mustard"
 	 Add your qualifications for major browser experience divisions here.
 	 For example, you might choose to only enhance browsers that support document.querySelector (IE8+, etc).
 	 Use case will vary.
 	 */
 	if (!( "querySelector" in doc && 'localStorage' in window && 'addEventListener' in window)) {
 		//if( !( "querySelector" in doc) ){
 		// basic browsers: last stop here!
 		return;
 	}
 
 	// From here on we're dealing with qualified browsers.
 
 	// Add scoping classes to HTML element: useful for upgrading the presentation of elements that will be enhanced with JS behavior
 	docElem.className += " " + htmlClasses.join(" ");
 
 	/* Load JavaScript enhancements in one request.
 	 Your DOM framework and dependent component scripts should be concatenated and minified into one file that we'll load dynamically (keep that file as small as possible!)
 	 A meta tag with a name matching the fullJSKey should have a content attribute referencing the path to this JavaScript file.
 	 */
 	var fullJS = getMeta(fullJSKey);
 	if (fullJS) {
 		loadJS(fullJS.content);
 	}
 
 	// expose the 'enhance' object globally. Use it to expose anything in here that's useful to other parts of your application.
 	window.enhance = enhance;
 
 }(this));

     <section class="themespage-take-action" id="section4498" style="background-image: url('/fileadmin/user_upload_bund/bilder/waelder/keepers_wald_fluss.jpg');">
      <h2 class="rte-heading rte-heading--h2 rte-heading__centered">
       Aktiv werden
      </h2>
      <div class="themespage-take-action--content">
       <div class="g-container">
        <div class="themespage-take-action--itemWrapper g-clearfix">
         <a class="themespage-take-action--item" href="/chemie/toxfox/">
          <img alt="" class="themespage-take-action--item__thumbnail" height="300" src="/fileadmin/_processed_/a/2/csm_tox_bubble_f64bead22b.jpg" width="300"/>
          <div class="themespage-take-action--item__titleWrapper">
           <h2 class="rte-heading rte-heading--h4 themespage-take-action--item__title">
            Schadstoffe aufdecken – mit dem ToxFox
           </h2>
          </div>
          <div class="themespage-take-action--item__overlay">
           <div class="themespage-take-action--item__overlayContent">
            <p class="rte-heading rte-heading--h4 themespage-take-action--item__title">
             Schadstoffe aufdecken – mit dem ToxFox
            </p>
            <p class="themespage-take-action--item__description">
             Barcode scannen – Gift erkennen: mit der ToxFox-App fürs iPhone bleibt Ihr Einkaufswagen frei von hormonellen Schadstoffen.
            </p>
           </div>
          </div>
         </a>

     <section class="m-layout-section m-layout-section__bottomPadding " id="section3897">
      <div class="g-container">
       <div class="m-layout-grid m-layout-grid__3col m-layout-grid__centeredGrid">
        <div class=" " id="c5269">
         <h2 class="rte-heading ">
          BUND-Mitglied werden!
         </h2>
         <div class="ce-textpic ce-left ce-intext">
          <span class="rte-image rte-image__imageLeft ">
           <span class="rte-image--imageWrapper">
            <a href="https://mitglied.bund.net/?wc=21731" target="_blank">
             <img alt="Fleischatlas 2018" class="rte-image--image" src="/fileadmin/user_upload_bund/bilder/startseite/fleischatlas_cover.jpg" title="Fleischatlas 2018. Foto: BUND"/>
            </a>
           </span>
           <span class="rte-paragraph rte-paragraph__caption rte-image--imageCaption">
           </span>
          </span>
          <div class="ce-bodytext">
           <p>
            Wie kann eine tier- und verbraucher­freundliche Agrarwende organisiert werden? Jetzt BUND-Mitglied werden und den Fleischatlas 2018 als Dankeschön erhalten!
           </p>
           <p>
            <a class="rte-anchor rte-anchor--button rte-anchor--button__btnGreen" href="https://mitglied.bund.net/?wc=21731" target="_blank">
             Hier geht's zur Ihrer Mitgliedschaft
            </a>
           </p>
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>
        <div class=" " id="c4933">
         <h2 class="rte-heading ">
          BUNDladen
         </h2>
         <div class="ce-textpic ce-left ce-intext">
          <span class="rte-image rte-image__imageLeft ">
           <span class="rte-image--imageWrapper">
            <a href="https://www.bundladen.de/Tierwelt/Voegel/Nisthilfen/Bausatz-fuer-einen-Meisenkasten.html" target="_blank">
             <img alt="Meisenkasten. Foto: BUNDladen" class="rte-image--image" src="/fileadmin/user_upload_bund/bilder/startseite/meisenkasten.jpg" title="Meisenkasten. Foto: BUNDladen"/>
            </a>
           </span>
           <span class="rte-paragraph rte-paragraph__caption rte-image--imageCaption">
           </span>
          </span>
          <div class="ce-bodytext">
           <p>
            Mit einem Nistkas- ten-Set aus dem BUNDladen bauen Sie der Stadtmeise eine Bleibe und bekommen eine kleine Vogelfamilie als Nachbarn.
           </p>
           <p>
            <a class="rte-anchor rte-anchor--button rte-anchor--button__btnGreen" href="https://www.bundladen.de/Tierwelt/Voegel/Nisthilfen/Bausatz-fuer-einen-Meisenkasten.html" target="_blank">
             Zum BUNDladen
            </a>

         </div>

          BUND-Leitbild
         </h2>
         <div class="ce-textpic ce-left ce-intext">
          <span class="rte-image rte-image__imageLeft ">
           <span class="rte-image--imageWrapper">

          </span>

           <p>
            Der BUND versteht sich als die trei­bende gesell­schaftliche Kraft für eine nachhaltige Entwicklung in Deutschland. Er will ein zukunftsfähiges Land in einer friedfertigen Welt.
           </p>
           <p>

         <h2 class="rte-heading ">
          Landesverbände
         </h2>
         <div class="ce-textpic ce-left ce-intext">
          <span class="rte-image rte-image__imageLeft ">
           <span class="rte-image--imageWrapper">
            <a href="/ueber-uns/organisation/landesverbaende/">
             <img alt="" class="rte-image--image" src="/fileadmin/user_upload_bund/bilder/startseite/lv_start_neu.jpg" title=""/>
            </a>
           </span>
           <span class="rte-paragraph rte-paragraph__caption rte-image--imageCaption">
           </span>
          </span>
          <div class="ce-bodytext">
           <p>
            Der BUND ist föderativ orga­nisiert: In jedem Bundesland engagiert sich  ein BUND-Lan­des­­verband für Natur- und Umweltschutz. Erfahren Sie mehr über die regionalen Verbände.
           </p>
           <p>
            <a class="rte-anchor rte-anchor--button rte-anchor--button__btnGreen" href="/ueber-uns/organisation/landesverbaende/">
             Zur Übersicht
            </a>
           </p>
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>

         </h2>
         <div class="ce-textpic ce-left ce-intext">
          <span class="rte-image rte-image__imageLeft ">
           <span class="rte-image--imageWrapper">
            <a href="/spenden-und-unterstuetzen/weitere-moeglichkeiten/bundstiftung/">

           <span class="rte-paragraph rte-paragraph__caption rte-image--imageCaption">
           </span>
          </span>
          <div class="ce-bodytext">
           <p>
            Mit der BUNDstiftung möchten wir erreichen, dass natürlicher Wildwuchs wieder zum wesentlichen Faktor in  unserer Landschaft wird!
           </p>
           <p>
            <a class="rte-anchor rte-anchor--button rte-anchor--button__btnGreen" href="/spenden-und-unterstuetzen/weitere-moeglichkeiten/bundstiftung/">

 /*_scriptCode*/
 
 			// decrypt helper function
 		function decryptCharcode(n,start,end,offset) {
 			n = n + offset;
 			if (offset > 0 && n > end) {
 				n = start + (n - end - 1);
 			} else if (offset < 0 && n < start) {
 				n = end - (start - n - 1);
 			}
 			return String.fromCharCode(n);
 		}
 			// decrypt string
 		function decryptString(enc,offset) {
 			var dec = "";
 			var len = enc.length;
 			for(var i=0; i < len; i++) {
 				var n = enc.charCodeAt(i);
 				if (n >= 0x2B && n <= 0x3A) {
 					dec += decryptCharcode(n,0x2B,0x3A,offset);	// 0-9 . , - + / :
 				} else if (n >= 0x40 && n <= 0x5A) {
 					dec += decryptCharcode(n,0x40,0x5A,offset);	// A-Z @
 				} else if (n >= 0x61 && n <= 0x7A) {
 					dec += decryptCharcode(n,0x61,0x7A,offset);	// a-z
 				} else {
 					dec += enc.charAt(i);
 				}
 			}
 			return dec;
 		}
 			// decrypt spam-protected emails
 		function linkTo_UnCryptMailto(s) {
 			location.href = decryptString(s,-1);
 		}

 document.createElement( 'picture' );/*! EnhanceJS: a progressive enhancement boilerplate. Copyright 2014 @scottjehl, Filament Group, Inc. Licensed MIT */
 (function (window, undefined) {
 
 	// Enable JS strict mode
 	"use strict";
 	var setTimeout = window.setTimeout;
 
 	var enhance = {};
 
 	// Define some variables to be used throughout this file
 	var doc = window.document,
 		docElem = doc.documentElement,
 		head = doc.head || doc.getElementsByTagName("head")[0],
 	// this references a meta tag's name whose content attribute should define the path to the full CSS file for the site
 		fullCSSKey = "fullcss",
 	// this references a meta tag's name whose content attribute should define the path to the enhanced JS file for the site (delivered to qualified browsers)
 		fullJSKey = "fulljs",
 	// classes to be added to the HTML element in qualified browsers
 		htmlClasses = ["enhanced"];
 
 	/* Some commonly used functions - delete anything you don't need! */
 
 	// loadJS: load a JS file asynchronously. Included from https://github.com/filamentgroup/loadJS/
 	function loadJS(src) {
 		var ref = window.document.getElementsByTagName("script")[0];
 		var script = window.document.createElement("script");
 		script.src = src;
 		script.async = true;
 		ref.parentNode.insertBefore(script, ref);
 		return script;
 	}
 
 	// expose it
 	enhance.loadJS = loadJS;
 
 	// loadCSS: load a CSS file asynchronously. Included from https://github.com/filamentgroup/loadCSS/
 	function loadCSS(href, before, media) {
 		// Arguments explained:
 		// `href` is the URL for your CSS file.
 		// `before` optionally defines the element we'll use as a reference for injecting our <link>
 		// By default, `before` uses the first <script> element in the page.
 		// However, since the order in which stylesheets are referenced matters, you might need a more specific location in your document.
 		// If so, pass a different reference element to the `before` argument and it'll insert before that instead
 		// note: `insertBefore` is used instead of `appendChild`, for safety re: http://www.paulirish.com/2011/surefire-dom-element-insertion/
 		var ss = window.document.createElement("link");
 		var ref = before || window.document.getElementsByTagName("script")[0];
 		var sheets = window.document.styleSheets;
 		ss.rel = "stylesheet";
 		ss.href = href;
 		// temporarily, set media to something non-matching to ensure it'll fetch without blocking render
 		ss.media = "only x";
 		// inject link
 		ref.parentNode.insertBefore(ss, ref);
 		// This function sets the link's media back to `all` so that the stylesheet applies once it loads
 		// It is designed to poll until document.styleSheets includes the new sheet.
 		function toggleMedia() {
 			var defined;
 			for (var i = 0; i < sheets.length; i++) {
 				if (sheets[i].href && sheets[i].href.indexOf(href) > -1) {
 					defined = true;
 				}
 			}
 			if (defined) {
 				ss.media = media || "all";
 			}
 			else {
 				setTimeout(toggleMedia);
 			}
 		}
 
 		toggleMedia();
 		return ss;
 	}
 
 	// expose it
 	enhance.loadCSS = loadCSS;
 
 	// getMeta function: get a meta tag by name
 	// NOTE: meta tag must be in the HTML source before this script is included in order to guarantee it'll be found
 	function getMeta(metaname) {
 		var metas = window.document.getElementsByTagName("meta");
 		var meta;
 		for (var i = 0; i < metas.length; i++) {
 			if (metas[i].name && metas[i].name === metaname) {
 				meta = metas[i];
 				break;
 			}
 		}
 		return meta;
 	}
 
 	// expose it
 	enhance.getMeta = getMeta;
 
 	// cookie function from https://github.com/filamentgroup/cookie/
 	function cookie(name, value, days) {
 		var expires;
 		// if value is undefined, get the cookie value
 		if (value === undefined) {
 			var cookiestring = "; " + window.document.cookie;
 			var cookies = cookiestring.split("; " + name + "=");
 			if (cookies.length == 2) {
 				return cookies.pop().split(";").shift();
 			}
 			return null;
 		}
 		else {
 			// if value is a false boolean, we'll treat that as a delete
 			if (value === false) {
 				days = -1;
 			}
 			if (days) {
 				var date = new Date();
 				date.setTime(date.getTime() + ( days * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000 ));
 				expires = "; expires=" + date.toGMTString();
 			}
 			else {
 				expires = "";
 			}
 			window.document.cookie = name + "=" + value + expires + "; path=/";
 		}
 	}
 
 	// expose it
 	enhance.cookie = cookie;
 
 	/* Enhancements for all browsers - qualified or not */
 
 	/* Load non-critical CSS async on first visit:
 	 On first visit to the site, the critical CSS for each template should be inlined in the head, while the full CSS for the site should be requested async and cached for later use.
 	 A meta tag with a name matching the fullCSSKey should have a content attribute referencing the path to the full CSS file for the site.
 	 If no cookie is set to specify that the full CSS has already been fetched, load it asynchronously and set the cookie.
 	 Once the cookie is set, the full CSS is assumed to be in cache, and the server-side templates should reference the full CSS directly from the head of the page with a link element, in place of inline critical styles.
 	 */
 	var fullCSS = getMeta(fullCSSKey);
 	if (fullCSS && !cookie(fullCSSKey)) {
 		loadCSS(fullCSS.content);
 		// set cookie to mark this file fetched
 		cookie(fullCSSKey, "true", 7);
 	}
 
 	/* Enhancements for qualified browsers - "Cutting the Mustard"
 	 Add your qualifications for major browser experience divisions here.
 	 For example, you might choose to only enhance browsers that support document.querySelector (IE8+, etc).
 	 Use case will vary.
 	 */
 	if (!( "querySelector" in doc && 'localStorage' in window && 'addEventListener' in window)) {
 		//if( !( "querySelector" in doc) ){
 		// basic browsers: last stop here!
 		return;
 	}
 
 	// From here on we're dealing with qualified browsers.
 
 	// Add scoping classes to HTML element: useful for upgrading the presentation of elements that will be enhanced with JS behavior
 	docElem.className += " " + htmlClasses.join(" ");
 
 	/* Load JavaScript enhancements in one request.
 	 Your DOM framework and dependent component scripts should be concatenated and minified into one file that we'll load dynamically (keep that file as small as possible!)
 	 A meta tag with a name matching the fullJSKey should have a content attribute referencing the path to this JavaScript file.
 	 */
 	var fullJS = getMeta(fullJSKey);
 	if (fullJS) {
 		loadJS(fullJS.content);
 	}
 
 	// expose the 'enhance' object globally. Use it to expose anything in here that's useful to other parts of your application.
 	window.enhance = enhance;
 
 }(this));

     <div class="m-intro-home js-m-intro-home">
      <article class="m-intro-home__item">
       <div class="m-intro-home__background" style="background-image: url('/fileadmin/user_upload_bund/bilder/startseite/wasser_kampagne_slider.jpg')">
       </div>
       <div class="m-intro-home__content">
        <h2 class="m-intro-home__headline ">
         Rette unser Wasser!
        </h2>
        <p class="rte-paragraph rte-paragraph__intro">
         Unser Wasser ist in akuter Gefahr: Die mächtige Lobby von Agrarchemie und Industrie will den EU-Wasserschutz schwächen. Das darf nicht passieren. Schicken Sie jetzt eine Nachricht an Bundesumweltministerin Schulze!
        </p>
        <p class="rte-paragraph rte-paragraph__intro">
         <a class="rte-anchor rte-anchor--button rte-anchor--button__btnRed" href="https://aktion.bund.net/rette-unser-wasser?utm_source=website&amp;utm_content=slider&amp;utm_campaign=WRRL&amp;utm_medium=website" target="_blank">
          Jetzt mitmachen!
         </a>
        </p>
       </div>
      </article>
      <article class="m-intro-home__item">
       <div class="m-intro-home__background" style="background-image: url('/fileadmin/user_upload_bund/bilder/startseite/kohle-stoppen.jpg')">
       </div>
       <div class="m-intro-home__content">
        <h2 class="m-intro-home__headline ">
         Demo: Stop Kohle!
        </h2>
        <p class="rte-paragraph rte-paragraph__intro">
         Das Endspiel um die Kohle beginnt. Am 24. Juni senden wir mit unseren Händen ein klares Signal: Stop Kohle! Gemeinsam zeigen wir: Die übergroße Mehrheit der Bevölkerung will beim Klimaschutz endlich Taten sehen.
        </p>
        <p class="rte-paragraph rte-paragraph__intro">
         <a class="rte-anchor rte-anchor--button rte-anchor--button__btnWhite" href="/service/termine/detail/event/demo-stop-kohle/">
          Mehr...
         </a>
        </p>
       </div>
      </article>
      <article class="m-intro-home__item">

       </div>
       <div class="m-intro-home__content">
        <h2 class="m-intro-home__headline ">
         Schmetterlinge beobachten
        </h2>
        <p class="rte-paragraph rte-paragraph__intro">
         Bei uns finden Sie Tipps, wie Sie unsere Falter beobachten und schützen können.
        </p>
        <p class="rte-paragraph rte-paragraph__intro">
         <a class="rte-anchor rte-anchor--button rte-anchor--button__btnWhite" href="/tiere-pflanzen/schmetterlinge/">

         </a>
        </p>

     <section class="m-layout-section m-layout-section__bottomPadding m-layout-section__backgroundLightGrey" id="section4396">
      <div class="g-container">
       <div class="m-content-donationslider ">
        <div class="m-content-donationslider--sliderWrapper">
         <div class="m-content-donationslider--sliderItem">
          <img class="m-content-donationslider--image" src="/fileadmin/user_upload_bund/bilder/startseite/sommertipps_teaser.jpg"/>
          <h2 class="rte-heading rte-heading--h3">
           Unsere Sommertipps
          </h2>
          <p class="rte-paragraph">
           So wird der Sommer noch schöner: Mit unseren Sommertipps lernen Sie u.a., wie Sie umweltfreundlich grillen, Sonnenbrand auf natürliche Weise vorbeugen oder ungetrübt in Seen und Flüssen baden können.
          </p>
          <a class="rte-anchor rte-anchor--button rte-anchor--button__btnGreen rte-anchor--button__btnBlock" href="https://www.bund.net/bund-tipps/oekotipps/tip-topic/sommer/" target="_self">
           Weiterlesen
          </a>
         </div>
         <div class="m-content-donationslider--sliderItem">
          <img class="m-content-donationslider--image" src="/fileadmin/user_upload_bund/bilder/startseite/bienen_start.jpg"/>
          <h2 class="rte-heading rte-heading--h3">
           A Place to Bee
          </h2>
          <p class="rte-paragraph">
           Mit 3.500 Häkelbienen im Gepäck haben wir mehr als 180.000 Unterschriften zum Schutz von Bienen und anderen Bestäubern an das Bundesumweltministerium übergeben. Nun ist die Politik am Zug.
          </p>
          <a class="rte-anchor rte-anchor--button rte-anchor--button__btnGreen rte-anchor--button__btnBlock" href="https://aktion.bund.net/a-place-to-bee" target="_blank">
           Weiterlesen
          </a>
         </div>
         <div class="m-content-donationslider--sliderItem">
          <img class="m-content-donationslider--image" src="/fileadmin/user_upload_bund/bilder/startseite/pestizidfreie_kommune_klein.jpg"/>
          <h2 class="rte-heading rte-heading--h3">
           Pestizidfreie Städte
          </h2>
          <p class="rte-paragraph">
           Bisher haben sich 210 Städte und Gemeinden entschieden, ihre Grünflächen ohne Pestizide oder mindestens ohne Glyphosat zu bewirtschaften. Wir haben eine interaktive Karte dieser Orte erstellt.
          </p>
          <a class="rte-anchor rte-anchor--button rte-anchor--button__btnGreen rte-anchor--button__btnBlock" href="/umweltgifte/pestizide/pestizidfreie-kommune/">
           weiterlesen
          </a>
         </div>
         <div class="m-content-donationslider--sliderItem">
          <img class="m-content-donationslider--image" src="/fileadmin/_processed_/2/7/csm_denkmal_aktiv_schueler_unterricht_4be4e52150.jpg"/>
          <h2 class="rte-heading rte-heading--h3">
           BUND-Umweltbildung
          </h2>
          <p class="rte-paragraph">
           Bildung ist ein zentraler Aspekt erfolgreicher Umweltarbeit. Im Fokus des BUND steht die Bildung für nachhaltige Entwicklung – für jede Altersstufe. Erfahren Sie mehr über unsere Projekte in der Umweltbildung!
          </p>
          <a class="rte-anchor rte-anchor--button rte-anchor--button__btnGreen rte-anchor--button__btnBlock" href="/bund-tipps/natur-erfahren/umweltbildung/">
           Weiterlesen
          </a>
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </section>

         <h2 class="rte-heading ">
          BUND-Mitglied werden!
         </h2>
         <div class="ce-textpic ce-left ce-intext">
          <span class="rte-image rte-image__imageLeft ">
           <span class="rte-image--imageWrapper">
            <a href="https://mitglied.bund.net/?wc=21731" target="_blank">

           </span>
          </span>

           <p>
            Wie kann eine tier- und verbraucher­freundliche Agrarwende organisiert werden? Jetzt BUND-Mitglied werden und den Fleischatlas 2018 als Dankeschön erhalten!
           </p>
           <p>
            <a class="rte-anchor rte-anchor--button rte-anchor--button__btnGreen" href="https://mitglied.bund.net/?wc=21731" target="_blank">
             Hier geht's zur Ihrer Mitgliedschaft
            </a>
           </p>

           </p>

            <a class="rte-anchor rte-anchor--button rte-anchor--button__btnGreen" href="https://www.bundladen.de/Tierwelt/Voegel/Nisthilfen/Bausatz-fuer-einen-Meisenkasten.html" target="_blank">

            <a class="rte-anchor rte-anchor--button rte-anchor--button__btnGreen" href="/service/newsletter/">
             BUND-Newsletter abonnieren

         </div>

        <div class=" " id="c6567">
         <h2 class="rte-heading ">
          BUND-Leitbild
         </h2>
         <div class="ce-textpic ce-left ce-intext">
          <span class="rte-image rte-image__imageLeft ">
           <span class="rte-image--imageWrapper">
            <a href="/ueber-uns/transparenz/leitbild/">
             <img alt="" class="rte-image--image" src="/fileadmin/user_upload_bund/bilder/bund/leuchtturm_leitbild.jpg" title="Leuchtturm; Foto: Joshua Hibbert / unsplash.com"/>
            </a>
           </span>
           <span class="rte-paragraph rte-paragraph__caption rte-image--imageCaption">
           </span>
          </span>
          <div class="ce-bodytext">
           <p>
            Der BUND versteht sich als die trei­bende gesell­schaftliche Kraft für eine nachhaltige Entwicklung in Deutschland. Er will ein zukunftsfähiges Land in einer friedfertigen Welt.
           </p>
           <p>
            <a class="rte-anchor rte-anchor--button rte-anchor--button__btnGreen" href="/ueber-uns/transparenz/leitbild/">

         </h2>
         <div class="ce-textpic ce-left ce-intext">

            </a>
           </span>
           <span class="rte-paragraph rte-paragraph__caption rte-image--imageCaption">
           </span>
          </span>
          <div class="ce-bodytext">
           <p>
            Eine Natur ohne Insekten ist undenkbar. Doch ihre Zahl ist in den letzten Jahrzehnten stark gesunken. Wir müssen mehr tun für Bienen, Käfer und Co.
           </p>
           <p>
            <a class="rte-anchor rte-anchor--button rte-anchor--button__btnGreen" href="/service/publikationen/bundmagazin/">

    /*<![CDATA[*/
 /*_scriptCode*/
 
 			// decrypt helper function
 		function decryptCharcode(n,start,end,offset) {
 			n = n + offset;
 			if (offset > 0 && n > end) {
 				n = start + (n - end - 1);
 			} else if (offset < 0 && n < start) {
 				n = end - (start - n - 1);
 			}
 			return String.fromCharCode(n);
 		}
 			// decrypt string
 		function decryptString(enc,offset) {
 			var dec = "";
 			var len = enc.length;
 			for(var i=0; i < len; i++) {
 				var n = enc.charCodeAt(i);
 				if (n >= 0x2B && n <= 0x3A) {
 					dec += decryptCharcode(n,0x2B,0x3A,offset);	// 0-9 . , - + / :
 				} else if (n >= 0x40 && n <= 0x5A) {
 					dec += decryptCharcode(n,0x40,0x5A,offset);	// A-Z @
 				} else if (n >= 0x61 && n <= 0x7A) {
 					dec += decryptCharcode(n,0x61,0x7A,offset);	// a-z
 				} else {
 					dec += enc.charAt(i);
 				}
 			}
 			return dec;
 		}
 			// decrypt spam-protected emails
 		function linkTo_UnCryptMailto(s) {
 			location.href = decryptString(s,-1);
 		}

 	// loadJS: load a JS file asynchronously. Included from https://github.com/filamentgroup/loadJS/
 	function loadJS(src) {
 		var ref = window.document.getElementsByTagName("script")[0];
 		var script = window.document.createElement("script");
 		script.src = src;
 		script.async = true;
 		ref.parentNode.insertBefore(script, ref);
 		return script;
 	}
 
 	// expose it
 	enhance.loadJS = loadJS;
 
 	// loadCSS: load a CSS file asynchronously. Included from https://github.com/filamentgroup/loadCSS/
 	function loadCSS(href, before, media) {
 		// Arguments explained:
 		// `href` is the URL for your CSS file.
 		// `before` optionally defines the element we'll use as a reference for injecting our <link>
 		// By default, `before` uses the first <script> element in the page.
 		// However, since the order in which stylesheets are referenced matters, you might need a more specific location in your document.
 		// If so, pass a different reference element to the `before` argument and it'll insert before that instead
 		// note: `insertBefore` is used instead of `appendChild`, for safety re: http://www.paulirish.com/2011/surefire-dom-element-insertion/
 		var ss = window.document.createElement("link");
 		var ref = before || window.document.getElementsByTagName("script")[0];
 		var sheets = window.document.styleSheets;
 		ss.rel = "stylesheet";
 		ss.href = href;
 		// temporarily, set media to something non-matching to ensure it'll fetch without blocking render
 		ss.media = "only x";
 		// inject link
 		ref.parentNode.insertBefore(ss, ref);
 		// This function sets the link's media back to `all` so that the stylesheet applies once it loads
 		// It is designed to poll until document.styleSheets includes the new sheet.
 		function toggleMedia() {
 			var defined;
 			for (var i = 0; i < sheets.length; i++) {
 				if (sheets[i].href && sheets[i].href.indexOf(href) > -1) {
 					defined = true;
 				}
 			}
 			if (defined) {
 				ss.media = media || "all";
 			}
 			else {
 				setTimeout(toggleMedia);
 			}
 		}
 
 		toggleMedia();
 		return ss;
 	}
 
 	// expose it
 	enhance.loadCSS = loadCSS;
 
 	// getMeta function: get a meta tag by name
 	// NOTE: meta tag must be in the HTML source before this script is included in order to guarantee it'll be found
 	function getMeta(metaname) {
 		var metas = window.document.getElementsByTagName("meta");
 		var meta;
 		for (var i = 0; i < metas.length; i++) {
 			if (metas[i].name && metas[i].name === metaname) {
 				meta = metas[i];
 				break;
 			}
 		}
 		return meta;
 	}
 
 	// expose it
 	enhance.getMeta = getMeta;
 
 	// cookie function from https://github.com/filamentgroup/cookie/
 	function cookie(name, value, days) {
 		var expires;
 		// if value is undefined, get the cookie value
 		if (value === undefined) {
 			var cookiestring = "; " + window.document.cookie;
 			var cookies = cookiestring.split("; " + name + "=");
 			if (cookies.length == 2) {
 				return cookies.pop().split(";").shift();
 			}
 			return null;
 		}
 		else {
 			// if value is a false boolean, we'll treat that as a delete
 			if (value === false) {
 				days = -1;
 			}
 			if (days) {
 				var date = new Date();
 				date.setTime(date.getTime() + ( days * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000 ));
 				expires = "; expires=" + date.toGMTString();
 			}
 			else {
 				expires = "";
 			}
 			window.document.cookie = name + "=" + value + expires + "; path=/";
 		}
 	}
 
 	// expose it
 	enhance.cookie = cookie;
 
 	/* Enhancements for all browsers - qualified or not */
 
 	/* Load non-critical CSS async on first visit:
 	 On first visit to the site, the critical CSS for each template should be inlined in the head, while the full CSS for the site should be requested async and cached for later use.
 	 A meta tag with a name matching the fullCSSKey should have a content attribute referencing the path to the full CSS file for the site.
 	 If no cookie is set to specify that the full CSS has already been fetched, load it asynchronously and set the cookie.
 	 Once the cookie is set, the full CSS is assumed to be in cache, and the server-side templates should reference the full CSS directly from the head of the page with a link element, in place of inline critical styles.
 	 */
 	var fullCSS = getMeta(fullCSSKey);
 	if (fullCSS && !cookie(fullCSSKey)) {
 		loadCSS(fullCSS.content);
 		// set cookie to mark this file fetched
 		cookie(fullCSSKey, "true", 7);
 	}
 
 	/* Enhancements for qualified browsers - "Cutting the Mustard"
 	 Add your qualifications for major browser experience divisions here.
 	 For example, you might choose to only enhance browsers that support document.querySelector (IE8+, etc).
 	 Use case will vary.
 	 */
 	if (!( "querySelector" in doc && 'localStorage' in window && 'addEventListener' in window)) {
 		//if( !( "querySelector" in doc) ){
 		// basic browsers: last stop here!
 		return;
 	}
 
 	// From here on we're dealing with qualified browsers.
 
 	// Add scoping classes to HTML element: useful for upgrading the presentation of elements that will be enhanced with JS behavior
 	docElem.className += " " + htmlClasses.join(" ");
 
 	/* Load JavaScript enhancements in one request.
 	 Your DOM framework and dependent component scripts should be concatenated and minified into one file that we'll load dynamically (keep that file as small as possible!)
 	 A meta tag with a name matching the fullJSKey should have a content attribute referencing the path to this JavaScript file.
 	 */
 	var fullJS = getMeta(fullJSKey);
 	if (fullJS) {
 		loadJS(fullJS.content);
 	}
 
 	// expose the 'enhance' object globally. Use it to expose anything in here that's useful to other parts of your application.
 	window.enhance = enhance;

     <section class="m-layout-section m-layout-section__bottomPadding m-layout-section__backgroundLightGrey" id="section4396">
      <div class="g-container">
       <div class="m-content-donationslider ">
        <div class="m-content-donationslider--sliderWrapper">
         <div class="m-content-donationslider--sliderItem">
          <img class="m-content-donationslider--image" src="/fileadmin/user_upload_bund/bilder/startseite/sommertipps_teaser.jpg"/>
          <h2 class="rte-heading rte-heading--h3">
           Unsere Sommertipps
          </h2>
          <p class="rte-paragraph">
           So wird der Sommer noch schöner: Mit unseren Sommertipps lernen Sie u.a., wie Sie umweltfreundlich grillen, Sonnenbrand auf natürliche Weise vorbeugen oder ungetrübt in Seen und Flüssen baden können.
          </p>
          <a class="rte-anchor rte-anchor--button rte-anchor--button__btnGreen rte-anchor--button__btnBlock" href="https://www.bund.net/bund-tipps/oekotipps/tip-topic/sommer/" target="_self">
           Weiterlesen
          </a>
         </div>
         <div class="m-content-donationslider--sliderItem">
          <img class="m-content-donationslider--image" src="/fileadmin/user_upload_bund/bilder/startseite/bienen_start.jpg"/>
          <h2 class="rte-heading rte-heading--h3">
           A Place to Bee
          </h2>
          <p class="rte-paragraph">
           Mit 3.500 Häkelbienen im Gepäck haben wir mehr als 180.000 Unterschriften zum Schutz von Bienen und anderen Bestäubern an das Bundesumweltministerium übergeben. Nun ist die Politik am Zug.
          </p>
          <a class="rte-anchor rte-anchor--button rte-anchor--button__btnGreen rte-anchor--button__btnBlock" href="https://aktion.bund.net/a-place-to-bee" target="_blank">
           Weiterlesen
          </a>
         </div>
         <div class="m-content-donationslider--sliderItem">
          <img class="m-content-donationslider--image" src="/fileadmin/user_upload_bund/bilder/startseite/pestizidfreie_kommune_klein.jpg"/>
          <h2 class="rte-heading rte-heading--h3">
           Pestizidfreie Städte
          </h2>
          <p class="rte-paragraph">
           Bisher haben sich 210 Städte und Gemeinden entschieden, ihre Grünflächen ohne Pestizide oder mindestens ohne Glyphosat zu bewirtschaften. Wir haben eine interaktive Karte dieser Orte erstellt.
          </p>
          <a class="rte-anchor rte-anchor--button rte-anchor--button__btnGreen rte-anchor--button__btnBlock" href="/umweltgifte/pestizide/pestizidfreie-kommune/">
           weiterlesen
          </a>
         </div>
         <div class="m-content-donationslider--sliderItem">
          <img class="m-content-donationslider--image" src="/fileadmin/_processed_/2/7/csm_denkmal_aktiv_schueler_unterricht_4be4e52150.jpg"/>
          <h2 class="rte-heading rte-heading--h3">
           BUND-Umweltbildung
          </h2>
          <p class="rte-paragraph">
           Bildung ist ein zentraler Aspekt erfolgreicher Umweltarbeit. Im Fokus des BUND steht die Bildung für nachhaltige Entwicklung – für jede Altersstufe. Erfahren Sie mehr über unsere Projekte in der Umweltbildung!
          </p>
          <a class="rte-anchor rte-anchor--button rte-anchor--button__btnGreen rte-anchor--button__btnBlock" href="/bund-tipps/natur-erfahren/umweltbildung/">
           Weiterlesen
          </a>
         </div>

         <h2 class="rte-heading ">
          Landesverbände
         </h2>
         <div class="ce-textpic ce-left ce-intext">
          <span class="rte-image rte-image__imageLeft ">
           <span class="rte-image--imageWrapper">
            <a href="/ueber-uns/organisation/landesverbaende/">

           </span>
          </span>
          <div class="ce-bodytext">
           <p>
            Der BUND ist föderativ orga­nisiert: In jedem Bundesland engagiert sich  ein BUND-Lan­des­­verband für Natur- und Umweltschutz. Erfahren Sie mehr über die regionalen Verbände.
           </p>
